resolved map[uint64]struct{}, repeat time.Duration) bool {\\n670: \\t// If we haven't notified about the alert group before, notify right away\\n671: \\t// unless we only have resolved alerts.\\n672: \\tif entry == nil {\\n673: \\t\\treturn len(firing) > 0\\n674: \\t}\\n675: \\n676: \\tif !entry.IsFiringSubset(firing) {\\n677: \\t\\treturn true\\n678: \\t}\\n679: \\n680: \\t// Notify about all \\tr.metrics.numNotifications.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n778: \\tctx, alerts, err := r.exec(ctx, l, alerts...)\\n779: \\n780: \\tfailureReason := DefaultReason.String()\\n781: \\tif err \\tif entry == nil {\\n673: \\t\\treturn len(firing) > 0\\n674: \\t}\\n675: \\n676: \\tif !entry.IsFiringSubset(firing) {\\n677: \\t\\treturn true\\n678: \\t}\\n679: \\n680: \\t// Notify about all \\t\\t\\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n858: \\t\\t\\tif err != nil {\\n859: \\t\\t\\t\\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsFailedTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\\n860: \\t\\t\\t\\tif !retry {\\n861: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\treturn ctx, alerts, fmt.Errorf(\\\"%s/%s: notify time.Now().UTC()\n632: }\n633: \n634: // Wrap a slice in a struct so we can store a pointer in sync.Pool.\n635: type hashBuffer struct {\n636: \tbuf []byte\n637: }\n638: \n639: var hashBuffers = sync.Pool{\n640: \tNew: func() interface{} { return &hashBuffer{buf: make([]byte, 0, 1024)} },\n641: }\n642: \n643: func hashAlert(a *types.Alert) uint64 {\n644: \tconst sep = '\\xff'\n645: \n646: \thb := hashBuffers.Get().(*hashBuffer)\n647: \tdefer hashBuffers.Put(hb)\n648: \tb := hb.buf[:0]\n649: \n650: \tnames := make(model.LabelNames, 0, len(a.Labels))\n651: \n652: \tfor ln := range a.Labels {\n653: \t\tnames = append(names, ln)\n654: \t}\n655: \tsort.Sort(names)\n656: \n657: \tfor _, ln := range names {\n658: \t\tb = append(b, string(ln)...)\n659: \t\tb = append(b, sep)\n660: \t\tb = append(b, string(a.Labels[ln])...)\n661: \t\tb = append(b, sep)\n662: \t}\n663: \n664: \thash := xxhash.Sum64(b)\n665: \n666: \treturn hash\n667: }\n668: \n669: func (n *DedupStage) needsUpdate(entry *nflogpb.Entry, firing, resolved map[uint64]struct{}, repeat time.Duration) bool {\n670: \t// If we haven't notified about the alert group before, notify right away\n671: \t// unless we only have resolved alerts.\n672: \tif entry == nil {\n673: \t\treturn len(firing) > 0\n674: \t}\n675: \n676: \tif !entry.IsFiringSubset(firing) {\n677: \t\treturn true\n678: \t}\n679: \n680: \t// Notify about all alerts being resolved.\n681: \t// This is done irrespective of the send_resolved flag to make sure that\n682: \t// the firing alerts are cleared from the notification log.\n683: \tif len(firing) == 0 {\n684: \t\t// If the current alert group and last notification contain no firing\n685: \t\t// alert, it means that some alerts have been fired and resolved during the\n686: \t\t// last interval. In this case, there is no need to notify the receiver\n687: \t\t// since it doesn't know about them.\n688: \t\treturn len(entry.FiringAlerts) > 0\n689: \t}\n690: \n691: \tif n.rs.SendResolved() && !entry.IsResolvedSubset(resolved) {\n692: \t\treturn true\n693: \t}\n694: \n695: \t// Nothing changed, only notify if the repeat interval has passed.\n696: \treturn entry.Timestamp.Before(n.now().Add(-repeat))\n697: }\n698: \n699: // Exec implements the Stage interface.\n700: func (n *DedupStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, _ *slog.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n701: \tgkey, ok := GroupKey(ctx)\n702: \tif !ok {\n703: \t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"group key missing\")\n704: \t}\n705: \n706: \trepeatInterval, ok := RepeatInterval(ctx)\n707: \tif !ok {\n708: \t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"repeat interval missing\")\n709: \t}\n710: \n711: \tfiringSet := map[uint64]struct{}{}\n712: \tresolvedSet := map[uint64]struct{}{}\n713: \tfiring := []uint64{}\n714: \tresolved := []uint64{}\n715: \n716: \tvar hash uint64\n717: \tfor _, a := range alerts {\n718: \t\thash = n.hash(a)\n719: \t\tif a.Resolved() {\n720: \t\t\tresolved = append(resolved, hash)\n721: \t\t\tresolvedSet[hash] = struct{}{}\n722: \t\t} else {\n723: \t\t\tfiring = append(firing, hash)\n724: \t\t\tfiringSet[hash] = struct{}{}\n725: \t\t}\n726: \t}\n727: \n728: \tctx = WithFiringAlerts(ctx, firing)\n729: \tctx = WithResolvedAlerts(ctx, resolved)\n730: \n731: \tentries, err := n.nflog.Query(nflog.QGroupKey(gkey), nflog.QReceiver(n.recv))\n732: \tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, nflog.ErrNotFound) {\n733: \t\treturn ctx, nil, err\n734: \t}\n735: \n736: \tvar entry *nflogpb.Entry\n737: \tswitch len(entries) {\n738: \tcase 0:\n739: \tcase 1:\n740: \t\tentry = entries[0]\n741: \tdefault:\n742: \t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected entry result size %d\", len(entries))\n743: \t}\n744: \n745: \tif n.needsUpdate(entry, firingSet, resolvedSet, repeatInterval) {\n746: \t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n747: \t}\n748: \treturn ctx, nil, nil\n749: }\n750: \n751: // RetryStage notifies via passed integration with exponential backoff until it\n752: // succeeds. It aborts if the context is canceled or timed out.\n753: type RetryStage struct {\n754: \tintegration Integration\n755: \tgroupName   string\n756: \tmetrics     *Metrics\n757: \tlabelValues []string\n758: }\n759: \n760: // NewRetryStage returns a new instance of a RetryStage.\n761: func NewRetryStage(i Integration, groupName string, metrics *Metrics) *RetryStage {\n762: \tlabelValues := []string{i.Name()}\n763: \n764: \tif metrics.ff.EnableReceiverNamesInMetrics() {\n765: \t\tlabelValues = append(labelValues, i.receiverName)\n766: \t}\n767: \n768: \treturn &RetryStage{\n769: \t\tintegration: i,\n770: \t\tgroupName:   groupName,\n771: \t\tmetrics:     metrics,\n772: \t\tlabelValues: labelValues,\n773: \t}\n774: }\n775: \n776: func (r RetryStage) Exec(ctx context.Context, l *slog.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n777: \tr.metrics.numNotifications.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n778: \tctx, alerts, err := r.exec(ctx, l, alerts...)\n779: \n780: \tfailureReason := DefaultReason.String()\n781: \tif err != nil {\n782: \t\tvar e *ErrorWithReason\n783: \t\tif errors.As(err, &e) {\n784: \t\t\tfailureReason = \n791: func (r RetryStage) exec(ctx context.Context, l *slog.Logger, alerts ...*types.Alert) (context.Context, []*types.Alert, error) {\n792: \tvar sent []*types.Alert\n793: \n794: \t// If we shouldn't send notifications for resolved alerts, but there are only\n795: \t// resolved alerts, report them all as successfully notified (we still want the\n796: \t// notification log to log them for the next run of DedupStage).\n797: \tif !r.integration.SendResolved() {\n798: \t\tfiring, ok := FiringAlerts(ctx)\n799: \t\tif !ok {\n800: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, errors.New(\"firing alerts missing\")\n801: \t\t}\n802: \t\tif len(firing) == 0 {\n803: \t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n804: \t\t}\n805: \t\tfor _, a := range alerts {\n806: \t\t\tif a.Status() != model.AlertResolved {\n807: \t\t\t\tsent = append(sent, a)\n808: \t\t\t}\n809: \t\t}\n810: \t} else {\n811: \t\tsent = alerts\n812: \t}\n813: \n814: \tb := backoff.NewExponentialBackOff()\n815: \tb.MaxElapsedTime = 0 // Always retry.\n816: \n817: \ttick := backoff.NewTicker(b)\n818: \tdefer tick.Stop()\n819: \n820: \tvar (\n821: \t\ti    = 0\n822: \t\tiErr error\n823: \t)\n824: \n825: \tl = l.With(\"receiver\", r.groupName, \"integration\", r.integration.String())\n826: \tif groupKey, ok := GroupKey(ctx); ok {\n827: \t\tl = l.With(\"aggrGroup\", groupKey)\n828: \t}\n829: \n830: \tfor {\n831: \t\ti++\n832: \t\t// Always check the context first to not notify again.\n833: \t\tselect {\n834: \t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n835: \t\t\tif iErr == nil {\n836: \t\t\t\tiErr = ctx.Err()\n837: \t\t\t\tif errors.Is(iErr, context.Canceled) {\n838: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextCanceledReason, iErr)\n839: \t\t\t\t} else if errors.Is(iErr, context.DeadlineExceeded) {\n840: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextDeadlineExceededReason, iErr)\n841: \t\t\t\t}\n842: \t\t\t}\n843: \n844: \t\t\tif iErr != nil {\n845: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, iErr)\n846: \t\t\t}\n847: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n848: \t\tdefault:\n849: \t\t}\n850: \n851: \t\tselect {\n852: \t\tcase <-tick.C:\n853: \t\t\tnow := time.Now()\n854: \t\t\tretry, err := r.integration.Notify(ctx, sent...)\n855: \t\t\tdur := time.Since(now)\n856: \t\t\tr.metrics.notificationLatencySeconds.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Observe(dur.Seconds())\n857: \t\t\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n858: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n859: \t\t\t\tr.metrics.numNotificationRequestsFailedTotal.WithLabelValues(r.labelValues...).Inc()\n860: \t\t\t\tif !retry {\n861: \t\t\t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled due to unrecoverable error after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, err)\n862: \t\t\t\t}\n863: \t\t\t\tif ctx.Err() == nil {\n864: \t\t\t\t\tif iErr == nil || err.Error() != iErr.Error() {\n865: \t\t\t\t\t\t// Log the error if the context isn't done and the error isn't the same as before.\n866: \t\t\t\t\t\tl.Warn(\"Notify attempt failed, will retry later\", \"attempts\", i, \"err\", err)\n867: \t\t\t\t\t}\n868: \t\t\t\t\t// Save this error to be able to return the last seen error by an\n869: \t\t\t\t\t// integration upon context timeout.\n870: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = err\n871: \t\t\t\t}\n872: \t\t\t} else {\n873: \t\t\t\tl := l.With(\"attempts\", i, \"duration\", dur)\n874: \t\t\t\tif i <= 1 {\n875: \t\t\t\t\tl = l.With(\"alerts\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", alerts))\n876: \t\t\t\t\tl.Debug(\"Notify success\")\n877: \t\t\t\t} else {\n878: \t\t\t\t\tl.Info(\"Notify success\")\n879: \t\t\t\t}\n880: \n881: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, alerts, nil\n882: \t\t\t}\n883: \t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n884: \t\t\tif iErr == nil {\n885: \t\t\t\tiErr = ctx.Err()\n886: \t\t\t\tif errors.Is(iErr, context.Canceled) {\n887: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextCanceledReason, iErr)\n888: \t\t\t\t} else if errors.Is(iErr, context.DeadlineExceeded) {\n889: \t\t\t\t\tiErr = NewErrorWithReason(ContextDeadlineExceededReason, iErr)\n890: \t\t\t\t}\n891: \t\t\t}\n892: \t\t\tif iErr != nil {\n893: \t\t\t\treturn ctx, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"%s/%s: notify retry canceled after %d attempts: %w\", r.groupName, r.integration.String(), i, iErr)\n894: \t\t\t}\n895: \t\t\treturn ctx, nil, nil\n896: \t\t}\n897: \t}\n898: }\n899: \n900: // SetNotifiesStage sets the notification information about passed alerts. The\n901: // passed alerts should have already been sent to the receivers.\n902: type SetNotifiesStage struct {\n903: \tnflog NotificationLog\n904: \trecv  *nflogpb.Receiver\n905: }\n906: \n907: //
